	eventsequence "StepSmoke"
	{
		particleType		= PT_3D_PLANE
		Layer				= 35
		sourceblendmode		= D3DBLEND_SRCALPHA
		destblendmode		= D3DBLEND_INVSRCALPHA
		numparticles		= 50
		gravity			= XYZ(0,0,0)
		emitradius		= XYZ(random(-50,50),20,random(-50,50))
                lifetime		= 1

		initial                 texture		= "smoke.dds"
		initial			color		= rgba(1,1,1,0.9)
		fade so final	        color		= rgba(1,1,1,0)
		initial			size		= XYZ(60,60,1)
		fade so final	        size		= XYZ(30,30,1)
		initial			rotate		= XYZ(0,0,random(-45,45))
		fade so final	        rotate		= XYZ(0,0,random(45,-45))
